## Padawan

## Historical information

### Established by

[Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi")[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1)

## Organizational information

### Organization

[Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order")[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1)

### Position type

Jedi rank[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1)

### Duties

[Jedi Commander](/wiki/Jedi_Commander "Jedi Commander") (during the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"))[[2]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-2)

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:TitleOrPosition)

:   "*Soon enough, you'll be making your own decisions out there in the galaxy as a Jedi Knight. You won't have to listen to me anymore.*"  
    "*I'm sure I'll always listen to you, master.*"  
    "*You'll always* hear *me, but that doesn't mean you'll always act exactly as I would. That's the journey of master and apprentice. My teachings should be something you* build on*, reinterpreted for yourself and the choices you have to make.*"
:   ―Jedi Master Luke Skywalker and his student Ben Solo[[3]](#cite_note-SW_2020_50-3)

A **Padawan**, also known as a **Padawan learner**, **Padawan apprentice**, **Jedi apprentice**, or **apprentice**, was the stage of [Jedi training](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") where a [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") trained under a [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") or [Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master"). A Padawan's master was meant to choose their apprentice, although, during the [galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") began to assign Padawans. In order to become a Knight, the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") in training needed to complete their [time](/wiki/Time "Time") as a Padawan and the [Trials](/wiki/Jedi_Trials "Jedi Trials").

During the Clone Wars, Padawans were trained in combat and served as [military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military") [commanders](/wiki/Jedi_Commander "Jedi Commander") of [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper"). At the end of the war, however, [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66") was enacted by [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), forcing the [clones](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") to turn on the Jedi Order. Still, some Jedi survived and, under the guidance of two survivors, Masters [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") and [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda"), [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker") was trained as a Jedi. Skywalker attempted to rebuild the Order, but the majority of his apprentices [were killed](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Destruction of the Jedi Temple") and [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo") turned to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"). Years later, [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker"), a [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger") from the [world](/wiki/Planet "Planet") of [Jakku](/wiki/Jakku "Jakku"), became the apprentice of Skywalker and later [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo").

## Overview[]

:   "*The boy. He your son?*"  
    "*No. He is my Padawan. Something between a student and an apprentice.*"
:   ―[Grecker](/wiki/Grecker "Grecker") and Obi-Wan Kenobi, discussing Anakin Skywalker[[4]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_and_Anakin_3-4)

 [![Padawan was a rank of the Jedi Order, given to apprentices who trained to become Jedi Knights.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c6/CalebDumeDepaBillabaTraining-Kanan1.png/revision/latest?cb=20160206054524) [![Padawan was a rank of the Jedi Order, given to apprentices who trained to become Jedi Knights.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c6/CalebDumeDepaBillabaTraining-Kanan1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160206054524)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c6/CalebDumeDepaBillabaTraining-Kanan1.png/revision/latest?cb=20160206054524) 

Padawan was a rank of the Jedi Order, given to apprentices who trained to become Jedi Knights.

 

A Padawan was a [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") who [trained](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") in the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") to one [day](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day") become a full-fledged [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi"). Padawans were known as [Jedi younglings](/wiki/Jedi_Initiate "Jedi Initiate") at first, and trained in classroom settings with multiple students and a teacher.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_II-5) Once they were ready for combat training and intensive study[[6]](#cite_note-VE-6) and reached a certain age, Padawans were normally apprenticed to a [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") or [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master"), beginning their one-on-one training.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1) Just as a Padawan learned from their master, often times the [teacher](/wiki/Teacher "Teacher") could learn from their student. Indeed, a master and apprentice needed to work together to be a true team and learning pair.[[7]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_&_Anakin-7) Padawan [Lily Tora-Asi](/wiki/Lily_Tora-Asi "Lily Tora-Asi") promised her master, Jedi Master [Arkoff](/wiki/Arkoff "Arkoff"), that she would go further than him and that she expected her own Padawan to follow suit by progressing even further than however she ended up.[[8]](#cite_note-Edge_of_Balance_1-8)

Much older than the typical youngling and almost rejected because of his age, [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") was welcomed into the Jedi Order at the age of nine. Immediately upon his initiation into the Order, he was named the Padawan learner to the newly-Knighted [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"). Despite his own experience as a young Padawan,[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1) Skywalker, during his days as a Jedi Knight, expressed surprise at[[2]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-2) the fourteen year old[[9]](#cite_note-DB:Ahsoka-9) [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano") being a Padawan, questioning whether she was old enough for the position. Indeed, Kenobi had at first assumed Tano to be a youngling when he first saw her.[[2]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-2) During the [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era"), the Jedi [Vernestra Rwoh](/wiki/Vernestra_Rwoh "Vernestra Rwoh") was a Padawan at a young age[[10]](#cite_note-Vern_DB-10) and so much of a prodigy[[11]](#cite_note-A_Test_of_Courage-11) that she was named a Jedi Knight at age fifteen, turning her into one of the youngest Knights in a generation. In fact, she would take on a Padawan of her own, [Imri Cantaros](/wiki/Imri_Cantaros "Imri Cantaros"), the following year.[[10]](#cite_note-Vern_DB-10)

No matter their experience or age, all Jedi generally associated [meditation](/wiki/Meditation "Meditation") with whoever had trained them; despite having been taught the basic principles of the matter during their [time](/wiki/Time "Time") as younglings, it was only after becoming a Padawan that a Jedi truly began to understand the process of meditation, spending time, ranging from [hours](/wiki/Standard_hour "Standard hour") to [weeks](/wiki/Standard_week "Standard week"), sitting next to their master in meditation to uncover the truths of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force"). As such times created an unbreakable bond, it was often the case that a Jedi, even if [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") had passed since they had last meditated with their master, would find the process difficult after their master [died](/wiki/Death "Death"). While it was indeed possible to recover and begin meditation again, the experience was never the same for the affected Jedi.[[12]](#cite_note-The_Rising_Storm-12)

 [![A Padawan would undertake missions alongside their master as part of their training.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/AnakinAhsokaFreefalling-DotD.png/revision/latest?cb=20120921025224) [![A Padawan would undertake missions alongside their master as part of their training.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/AnakinAhsokaFreefalling-DotD.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20120921025224)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/AnakinAhsokaFreefalling-DotD.png/revision/latest?cb=20120921025224) 

A Padawan would undertake missions alongside their master as part of their training.

 

A Jedi was meant to choose the Padawan whom they wished to train.[[13]](#cite_note-Front_Lines-13) Even though a Jedi could choose not to take on an apprentice, it was nevertheless considered part of a Jedi's responsibility to train the next generation of the Order.[[2]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-2) Apprentices would often go on missions with their masters as part of this one-on-one training. The [Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code") forbade a Jedi from training more than one Padawan or apprentice at a [time](/wiki/Time "Time"). Most of the Padawans were known to grow or wear [Padawan braids](/wiki/Padawan_braid "Padawan braid") to symbolize their rank. After completing the [Jedi Trials](/wiki/Jedi_Trials "Jedi Trials"), a Padawan would be promoted to the rank of Jedi Knight.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1) It was rare for a Padawan to not advance to the rank of Jedi Knight,[[14]](#cite_note-Padawan_Novel-14) but the struggles a Padawan faced on that journey, and the time it took to over come them, varied person-to-person.[[15]](#cite_note-The_Fallen_Star-15)

## History[]

### High Republic Era[]

#### Days of light[]

During the High Republic Era, a common training experience for Padawans was to be placed at a Jedi outpost alongside their master in the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories"), helping to uphold justice in the yet to be explored region. Nevertheless, they were sometimes given off-world assignments that took them away from the outpost.[[16]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-16) [Oliviah Zeveron](/wiki/Oliviah_Zeveron "Oliviah Zeveron") was a human Padawan apprenticed to the compassionate [Ugnaught](/wiki/Ugnaught "Ugnaught") Jedi Master [Fitan](/wiki/Fitan "Fitan"), who was a strong believer in the teachings of [Fin-So-Rowan](/wiki/Fin-So-Rowan "Fin-So-Rowan") and, thus, brought her Padawan with her across the galaxy on a mission to teach Jedi ways and [Luminous practices](/wiki/Doctrines_of_the_Luminous "Doctrines of the Luminous"). Zeveron loved the sense of adventure that came with their travels, over which they never seemed to stay still, experienced new worlds, and tried new [foods](/wiki/Foodstuff "Foodstuff"). In time, Zeveron tried to act mature and hide her excitement, but Fitan was able to break through her Padawan's veneer of seriousness.[[17]](#cite_note-PoV-17)

Jedi Master [Leebon](/wiki/Leebon "Leebon") permitted his Padawan, [Matthea Cathley](/wiki/Matthea_Cathley "Matthea Cathley"), an unprecedented level of independence for a Padawan. Listening to the Force, Cathley's training saw her studies consist of following the Force, leading to discoveries and misadventures that she was always happy to share with her master when she returned to their posting. Based on the Holy [Moon](/wiki/Moon "Moon") of [Jedha](/wiki/Jedha "Jedha"), Cathley called the [Temple of the Kyber](/wiki/Temple_of_the_Kyber "Temple of the Kyber") home because a proper [Jedi temple](/wiki/Jedi_temple "Jedi temple") did not exist on Jedha due to lingering [anti-Jedi sentiment](/wiki/Anti-Jedi_sentiment "Anti-Jedi sentiment") from the Order's past control over [Jedha City](/wiki/Jedha_City "Jedha City"). After those tensions exploded into the [Battle of Jedha](/wiki/Battle_of_Jedha "Battle of Jedha"), Leebon lost her life to the [Path of the Open Hand](/wiki/Path_of_the_Open_Hand "Path of the Open Hand"), so Jedi Master [Vildar Mac](/wiki/Vildar_Mac "Vildar Mac") took on Cathley as his Padawan so she could finish her training. By that time, Cathley's understanding of life as a Padawan had changed due to her experiences with Mac and their mutual friend [Tey Sirrek](/wiki/Tey_Sirrek "Tey Sirrek"), who both treated her as an equal. As such, she had a difficult working relationship with the then-Knight Zeveron, who treated her as an entry-level Padawan who should only speak when higher-ranking Jedi deemed it necessary, during their [mission to Dalna](/wiki/Mission_to_Dalna_(Sun_and_Forte) "Mission to Dalna (Sun and Forte)").[[17]](#cite_note-PoV-17)

#### Nihil conflict[]

 [![Padawan Bell Zettifar was trained by Jedi Master Loden Greatstorm.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/HRAAnnualHarvey.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211225201843) [![Padawan Bell Zettifar was trained by Jedi Master Loden Greatstorm.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/HRAAnnualHarvey.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20211225201843)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/HRAAnnualHarvey.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211225201843) 

Padawan Bell Zettifar was trained by Jedi Master Loden Greatstorm.

 

Padawan [Bell Zettifar](/wiki/Bell_Zettifar "Bell Zettifar") and his master, [Loden Greatstorm](/wiki/Loden_Greatstorm "Loden Greatstorm"), were stationed at the [Elphrona Outpost](/wiki/Elphrona_Outpost "Elphrona Outpost"). When they were meant to be rotated back to the [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") of [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"), [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Lina Soh](/wiki/Lina_Soh "Lina Soh") established a [hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace") [blockade](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade") due to the [Emergences](/wiki/Emergences "Emergences"), forcing the two Jedi to stay on [Elphrona](/wiki/Elphrona "Elphrona") for some [time](/wiki/Time "Time"). During the [Nihil](/wiki/Nihil "Nihil") [pirates](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate")' [raid on Elphrona](/wiki/Raid_on_Elphrona "Raid on Elphrona"), Greatstorm informed his apprentice that he was worthy of the title of Jedi Knight, but—after Greatstorm was captured by the Nihil—Zettifar refused to go through the Jedi Trials until he was rescued, wanting his mentor to attend the ceremony.[[16]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-16) In the aftermath of the [Battle of Grizal](/wiki/Battle_of_Grizal "Battle of Grizal"), during which the [Eye of the Nihil](/wiki/Eye_of_the_Nihil "Eye of the Nihil") [Marchion Ro](/wiki/Marchion_Ro "Marchion Ro") unleashed the [Great Leveler](/wiki/Great_Leveler "Great Leveler"), which turned Greatstorm to stone and left other Jedi on the battlefield, including Zettifar, mortified,[[12]](#cite_note-The_Rising_Storm-12) Jedi Padawans were asked to step up and help the Jedi Order in whatever way they could, just like the more experienced Knights and Jedi Masters. As such, a number of Padawans aboard the *[Starlight Beacon](/wiki/Starlight_Beacon "Starlight Beacon")* left to help defend the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_(Takodana) "Jedi Temple (Takodana)") of the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Takodana](/wiki/Takodana "Takodana") from a Nihil [|attack](/wiki/Battle_of_Takodana_(Nihil_conflict) "Battle of Takodana (Nihil conflict)").[[18]](#cite_note-HRA_8-18)

The stress of battles against the Nihil led to Masters [Torban Buck](/wiki/Torban_Buck "Torban Buck") and [Kantam Sy](/wiki/Kantam_Sy "Kantam Sy") re-establishing the "[Great Jedi Rumble Race](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Rumble_Race "Great Jedi Rumble Race")" for the Padawans of Starlight Beacon.[[19]](#cite_note-THRA_11-19) As the conflict carried on, Padawan [Ram Jomaram](/wiki/Ram_Jomaram "Ram Jomaram") found that masters were more willing to have their apprentices learn by "doing" and reasoned the previous generation of Jedi had not had the chance to take on as much duty as current Padawans needed to. He theorized to fellow Padawan [Reath Silas](/wiki/Reath_Silas "Reath Silas") that their mentors wanted the new generation to have an easier time during missions. Indeed, Silas's master, [Cohmac Vitus](/wiki/Cohmac_Vitus "Cohmac Vitus"), reflected to Sy that fighting dangers across the war-torn [Galactic Frontier](/wiki/Galactic_Frontier "Galactic Frontier") was not the life the two of them had been raised for.[[20]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-20)

### Fall of the Jedi[]

:   "*Master Yoda, I gave Qui-Gon my word. I will train Anakin. Without the approval of the council, if I must.*"  
    "*Qui-Gon's defiance I sense in you. Need that you do not. Agree with you the council does. Your apprentice Skywalker will be.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Yoda[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1)

 [![During the Clone Wars, Padawans served in the Grand Army of the Republic as Jedi Commanders.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/AhsokaBarriss-WF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111010231106) [![During the Clone Wars, Padawans served in the Grand Army of the Republic as Jedi Commanders.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/AhsokaBarriss-WF.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111010231106)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/AhsokaBarriss-WF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111010231106) 

During the Clone Wars, Padawans served in the Grand Army of the Republic as Jedi Commanders.

 

During the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") began to assign Padawans to Jedi Knights, instead of allowing them to choose.[[13]](#cite_note-Front_Lines-13) During the war, Padawans were trained in combat and forged into officers[[21]](#cite_note-Fall_of_Jedi_and_Order_66-21) of the [Republic Military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military") partly because of a lack of military leaders. Padawans held the rank of [Jedi Commander](/wiki/Jedi_Commander "Jedi Commander") and could lead forces of [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") as large as a [regiment](/wiki/Regiment "Regiment").[[22]](#cite_note-Rise-22) This led to cases where young and inexperienced Padawans, many of them still teenagers, outranked clone troopers with far more experience in combat. At the end of the conflict, in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"), Supreme Chancellor [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), secretly the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious, issued [Clone Protocol 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66"),[[23]](#cite_note-ROTS-23) forcing[[24]](#cite_note-Orders-24) the [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") to turn on their Jedi Generals and Commanders.[[23]](#cite_note-ROTS-23)

After the [establishment](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") of the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), a few ex-Padawans that had survived Order 66 or left the Jedi Order before the [purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") joined the nascent [Rebel Alliance](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic").[[25]](#cite_note-Dawn-25) This was the case of [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker")'s former apprentice, [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano"),[[26]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-26) as well as [Depa Billaba](/wiki/Depa_Billaba "Depa Billaba")'s former apprentice [Caleb Dume](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus"),[[27]](#cite_note-AND-27) who became known as Kanan Jarrus[[28]](#cite_note-Kanan_5-28) and later took on a Padawan of his own, [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger").[[29]](#cite_note-Spark_of_Rebellion-29) By [1 BBY](/wiki/1_BBY "1 BBY"),][[30]](#cite_note-Atlas-30) [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"), the [son](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") of Anakin Skywalker, began training under [Jedi Masters](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi")[[31]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-31) and later [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda").[[32]](#cite_note-Episode_V-32)

### Rebirth[]

:   "*Pass on what you have learned. Strength. Mastery. But weakness, folly, failure also. Yes, failure most of all. The greatest teacher, failure is. Luke, we are what they grow beyond. That is the true burden of all masters.*"
:   ―Yoda, to Luke Skywalker[[33]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-33)

 [![Luke Skywalker trained Rey as his final Jedi apprentice.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/Rey_TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20190830143748) [![Luke Skywalker trained Rey as his final Jedi apprentice.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/Rey_TLJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190830143748)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/Rey_TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20190830143748) 

Luke Skywalker trained Rey as his final Jedi apprentice.

 

Sometime after the [Liberation of Lothal](/wiki/Liberation_of_Lothal "Liberation of Lothal"), Ahsoka Tano took on [Sabine Wren](/wiki/Sabine_Wren "Sabine Wren") as her Padawan and taught her for a time.[[34]](#cite_note-Part_One-34) After the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor") in [4 ABY](/wiki/4_ABY "4 ABY"), which saw the deaths of both Emperor Palpatine and his apprentice Darth Vader, Skywalker attempted to rebuild the Jedi Order. However, his new generation of Jedi were killed by his nephew, [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo"), who fell to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"). Following this, Skywalker isolated himself to the [First Jedi Temple](/wiki/First_Jedi_Temple "First Jedi Temple") on the [Temple Island](/wiki/Temple_Island "Temple Island") on the distant planet of [Ahch-To](/wiki/Ahch-To "Ahch-To").[[35]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-35)

In [34 ABY](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY"),[[36]](#cite_note-Resistance_Reborn_Date-36) [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker"),[[33]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-33) a [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger")[[35]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-35) from [Jakku](/wiki/Jakku "Jakku"), arrived at the island to enlist him in the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance")'s [fight](/wiki/First_Order-Resistance_War "First Order-Resistance War") against the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order"), and later became his apprentice. Despite his misgivings about the Jedi Order, Skywalker trained her on the Temple Island and had his faith in the Jedi restored after a conversation with Yoda's [Force spirit](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit").[[33]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-33)

Following the [Battle of Crait](/wiki/Battle_of_Crait "Battle of Crait"), [General](/wiki/General "General") [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") introduced Rey to [Ambassador](/wiki/Ambassador "Ambassador") [Yendor Brethen](/wiki/Yendor_Brethen "Yendor Brethen") of [Ryloth](/wiki/Ryloth "Ryloth") as Skywalker's apprentice, which greatly impressed Brethen.[[37]](#cite_note-Resistance_Reborn-37) By the time of the return of Darth Sidious, in [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY"),[[38]](#cite_note-Date_Rise_of_Skywalker-38) Rey had begun training under Organa on [Ajan Kloss](/wiki/Ajan_Kloss "Ajan Kloss"), where the Resistance had established a secret [base](/wiki/Resistance_base_(Ajan_Kloss) "Resistance base (Ajan Kloss)"). Using her training, Rey would eventually go on to redeem Ben Solo and defeat Darth Sidious once and for all.[[39]](#cite_note-TROS-39)

## Behind the scenes[]

The term "Padawan" first written as "Padawaan" appeared as far back in [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas")'s first story treatments for the [1977](/wiki/1977 "1977") film [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"), then titled as *[Journal of the Whills](/wiki/Journal_of_the_Whills,_Part_I "Journal of the Whills, Part I")*.[[40]](#cite_note-The_Making_of_Star_Wars:_The_Definitive_Story_Behind_the_Original_Film-40) It wasn't heard, however, before the filming of the [1999](/wiki/1999 "1999") film [*Star Wars*: Episode I *The Phantom Menace*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace "Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace"), the first installment of the [prequel trilogy](/wiki/Prequel_trilogy "Prequel trilogy").[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1) In all previous works, including the original movies or early [*Star Wars* Legends](/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends "Star Wars Legends") stories, the concept was referred to as "Apprentice."

Set after the events of [*Star Wars*: Episode VI *Return of the Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VI_Return_of_the_Jedi "Star Wars: Episode VI Return of the Jedi"), the *[Star Wars: Trials on Tatooine](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Trials_on_Tatooine "Star Wars: Trials on Tatooine")* VR experience released by [ILMxLAB](/wiki/ILM_Immersive "ILM Immersive") featured an [unidentified hopeful Padawan](/wiki/Unidentified_hopeful_Padawan "Unidentified hopeful Padawan") who hoped to become part of Luke Skywalker's new Jedi Order. In an ensuing [mission to Tatooine](/wiki/Mission_to_Tatooine_(Hopeful_Padawan) "Mission to Tatooine (Hopeful Padawan)"), however, the Padawan found themself attacked by an Imperial remnant force. In the end, the Jedi would be victorious.[[41]](#cite_note-ToT-41)

38. [↑](#cite_ref-Date_Rise_of_Skywalker_38-0) *[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker:_The_Visual_Dictionary "Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary")* dates the events of *Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker* as taking place one [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") after the [Starkiller Incident](/wiki/Hosnian_Cataclysm "Hosnian Cataclysm"), which *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* dates to [34 ABY](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY"). Therefore, the events of *Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker*, including [Rey's](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker") [Jedi training](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") under [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"), must take place in [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY").
39. [↑](#cite_ref-TROS_39-0) [*Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IX_The_Rise_of_Skywalker "Star Wars: Episode IX The Rise of Skywalker")
40. [↑](#cite_ref-The_Making_of_Star_Wars:_The_Definitive_Story_Behind_the_Original_Film_40-0) *[The Making of Star Wars: The Definitive Story Behind the Original Film](/wiki/The_Making_of_Star_Wars:_The_Definitive_Story_Behind_the_Original_Film "The Making of Star Wars: The Definitive Story Behind the Original Film")*
41. [↑](#cite_ref-ToT_41-0) *[Star Wars: Trials on Tatooine](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Trials_on_Tatooine "Star Wars: Trials on Tatooine")*
